## [2.47.5](https://github.com/aodn/aodn-portal/tree/2.47.5) (2014-05-14)
[Full Changelog](https://github.com/aodn/aodn-portal/compare/3.16.0...2.47.5)

**Implemented enhancements:**

- Step 2 drop-down filters constrained by other drop-downs [\#1038](https://github.com/aodn/aodn-portal/issues/1038)
- Bounding box can be drawn for layers with no bbox filter configured [\#934](https://github.com/aodn/aodn-portal/issues/934)
- Replicate filter settings over multiple data collection with common filters [\#860](https://github.com/aodn/aodn-portal/issues/860)
- Temporal Extent "Displaying: date and time" on Step 2 [\#719](https://github.com/aodn/aodn-portal/issues/719)
- Hover over results shows abstract [\#548](https://github.com/aodn/aodn-portal/issues/548)
- Smart combo lists in 123 facets [\#531](https://github.com/aodn/aodn-portal/issues/531)
- Format WFS filters in a more user-friendly way [\#480](https://github.com/aodn/aodn-portal/issues/480)
- Poor screen usage in faceted search [\#260](https://github.com/aodn/aodn-portal/issues/260)
- Add Grails controller to handle client side error conditions [\#171](https://github.com/aodn/aodn-portal/issues/171)
- OpenID to work for other providers [\#108](https://github.com/aodn/aodn-portal/issues/108)
- Download cart enhancements [\#100](https://github.com/aodn/aodn-portal/issues/100)
